<td>Cadence is a popular DJ and she loves to dance. She opened the Night Club's <a href="/wiki/Dance_Contest" title="Dance Contest">Dance Contest</a> game <a href="/wiki/Dance-A-Thon" title="Dance-A-Thon"> in 2009</a>, where you can challenge your friends or dance solo.
